1497292172696< /time>
< Rating>
4<//Rating>
< review>
I'm not a Disney-phile, but I did enjoy my time at the local Disney Store.

Shockingly, the prices aren't bad here!  Being Disney, I expected price tags demanding beaucoup bucks.  However, most of the prices were reasonable, for the most part, and newborn/infant goods were 30% off.

The store has an attractive, easy to navigate layout, with Star Wars & Marvel immediately on the left, and princess merchandise on the right.  Seeing plush pillows of Yoda, Darth Vader & Spider-Man,  I can't deny I had an inkling to buy the whole lot of them.

On the right of the registers, an interactive area allows guests to watch movies, have storytime, play games & otherwise enjoy their Disney shopping experience.

Service was good.  The employees were quick to introduce themselves & ask if we needed any assistance.  We were only browsing, but it was great to feel welcome while we were there.

Being my first time in the store, I had an overall positive experience at my local Disney Store.  There are so many sickeningly cute & cuddly tchotchkes, it'll make your head spin.  Factor in competitive pricing, and the Disney Store becomes a top option for gifts, especially when it comes to Disney & Disneyland fans.

Highly recommend!< /review>

< Review>
I always try to support a local family-owned shop instead of a national chain whenever I can. I was getting ready to drive my car cross country back to the East coast and needed brand new suspension. The car had about 80,000 miles on it and was woefully in need of almost a complete suspension replacement including shocks, struts, stabilizer bars etc.. In addition I was due for a new set of tires. Anyone who's worked on a car from the East coast knows that we have particular ways to deal with rusty components as a result of the salt on the roads during winter. Generally if soaking it in WD-40 doesn't work, you bust out a torch and if that doesn't work then you break the part and replace it. Initially it looked like they weren't going to be able to fix one of the stabilizer bars without breaking it, but I asked them to have a little patience and let the WD-40 do its work overnight and the next day they were able to break it free and finish the alignment. The car drives like a dream now and the alignment is perfectly spot on. I just did about 60 miles of straight desert driving barely having to touch the steering wheel. The quality of the work was top-notch and worth the investment. The only constructive criticism I have is that they could do a slightly better job of communicating with customers, but then again the quality of the work is the most important thing to me.< /Review>

After going back and forth with Penske for the past couple months and having an attorney send a demand letter. We even pursued using the extended warranty which they say didn't cover any of the repairs needed to be done. So after calling our finance company Dakota Financial just to find out what was left on our loan of what we thought was a purchase and me bringing up the $9,333 down payment. We where told that that was not a down payment its a security deposit. The truck was listed at $29,000 with our insurance and extended warranty came up to about $31,000. Premier financing which is a separate entity from Penske, which I see today ironically has the same address as Penske 2675 Morgantown Rd Reading, PA 19607. Premier finance originally told us we were purchasing this truck that California had special laws and they had to write the contract up as such but they we are buying the truck. Dakota Financial said no we signed a lease agreement for 36 months at $1237 which adds up to $44,532 and at that point we can purchase the truck for $9,333 which brings up to total of $55,000. Had we known this we would have never 1. leased a used vehicle for this much 2. purchased a used truck for this much. I have emails from Premier asking for the downpayment which insinuate we were putting a down payment for purchasing this truck. Also on the cover sheet of Dakotas Financial agreement it states down payment as well. From what I read a down payment is for the purchase of property not a deposit for a lease. We have since yesterday already emailed them asking them if they are saying this is a lease that we want to return the truck to Dakota and get a full deposit and any money I've put out for current repairs. Without fixing the rest of the repairs that we can't afford this truck will be broke down for good in less than a month. The truck has been at the shop since April 5 2019 and we are supposed to get it back today if the over heating is fixed which I will have to pay about $3500 but none of the other issues I can fix. This truck was supposed to be a Premium truck not an as is truck. But it appears to be worth nothing.

So it sounds like this is a game all 3 companies have been running for a long time. We can't go after Penske but as per the contract this truck belongs to Dakota & Premier Financing is the one that sold this loan to us which I've attached an email I sent to them this morning. It looks like Penske left Dakota with a bad truck and Dakota financial had a bad sales man Premier Financing. Both Premier Financing and Dakota have ignored my emails. We would just like to return this lemon truck and get all of our money back. So we can try to get out of this bad title loan we took out on our already paid off car to get this truck. This truck was our only source of income for the time being and we have been without work for over a month now.

If you are mislead or deceived by this company you should file a report with the FTC, Consumer Financial Protection Bureau, the bbb, &  the DMV, a long with looking for the right lawyer to protect your rights.< /Text>

<Rating>1</Rating>< text>
Terrible place to do business with. Their "Lease agreement" as they call it, is their way of getting out of following the Truth in Lending Act. Most loan documents provide the original amount to be financed, length of terms, and payoff amount. Their "Lease Agreement" does none of this! They told my husband he has an Installment loan that has no interest....ha! The original amount to finance was $17,210. The agreement says $1012 a month for 36 months and thats it... nothing else! Well you do the math: $1012x36=$36,442...the original cost of the  semi was $37,210. I put it in an amortization schedule and the interest rate is 57.46368%. The maximum legal interest rate in CA is 10%. We're in Michigan and our maximum legal interest rate is 25%...like I said...their "Lease Agreement" jargon gets them around the Truth in Lending Act. Be very careful when considering this company!< /text>

<rating>5< /rating>< Text>
I am vision impaired and recently fell in the bedroom of our home.
My left arm and two middle fingers went numb.  At first I thought I had a bursitis problem.  However, the med's I take for that had no effect.
When the pain did not diminish, my wife suggested I call Dr. Ratkovic at Euclid Chiropractic.  We called and was able to get an appoint that same afternoon.
Using their in house X-Ray machine, Dr. Ratkovic took X-Rays and determined that I had hit the nerve bundle between my shoulder and spine.
The Dr. made an adjustment to my neck, used an ultrasound machine on the affected area then put ice on the area.
Before we left the office, I had response in my left arm and the two fingers that were numb.  I was told to put ice on the area for 10 to 15 minutes every hour or so, which I did.  By the next morning all the numbness was essentially gone.  However, we made a follow up appoint for that next day, just to make sure everything was OK.  It was and is and I'm back to work on my computer.
Although I do have bursitis from time to time I decided it was simpler to go have the problem diagnosed and fixed instead of guessing at what was going on instead of taking a lot of pain pills that hurt my stomach and don't take the pain away anyway.<//Text>
